 ) An Afghanistan batsman holds a unique record of first class cricket
 18 saal ke baheer shah apane pehle chaar pratham shrenee maichon main jabardast ballebaaji karte hue 207
 Has scored 831 runs with an average of 75
 first class kariyar ke shuruaati chaar maichon main sarvaadhik ran banane kii baat karen, to bashir ne australian diggaj bill ponsford ko peeche chhod diya he
 Ponsford had scored 741 runs in his first such matches
 first class cricket: baheer shah ke shuruaati 4 machapahala match - debyue main doharaa shatak (256*)teesraa match - donon pariyon main shatak(111 or 116)chauthaa match - tihara shatak (303*)raashid ke baad ab baheer shah ne chaunkaayarashid khan ke baad baheer shah ne cricket jagat kaa dhyaan apni ore khinchaa he
 Rashid Khan, known for his precise googly, made his debut at T20 International and One Day International in 2015
 us vakt ve 17 saal ke the
 Rashid has taken 63 wickets in 29 odis and 42 wickets in 27 T20 Internationals so far
 unhone june westeindies ke khilaaf 18 ran dekar 7 wicket chatkaaye
 His performance is the fourth best bowling in ODI history
 beete saptaah jab udyog or siyasat modi sarkaar ke pehle purna bajet ke intjaar main nakhun chaba rahe the, tab desh main kai or bajet bhi pesh ho rahe the
 India is not a budget but a country of 29 budgets and the time has come to take these 29 budgets of the states very seriously
 agle ek saal main bharat ke rajya us vittiya takat se las ho chuke honge, jo desh main aarthik nitiyon kaa hi nahin balki raajnneeti kaa cheharaa bhi badal degi
 As the French writer Victor Hugo used to say, no one can stop the idea whose time has come
 rajyon ko aarthik faislon kii aazaadee or sansaadhan dene kaa samay aa gaya tha isliye ise roka nahin ja sakaa
 You can call it the most far-reaching economic reform of India, which has quietly come amidst the political outcry of the last decade
 narendra modi ke satta main aane se pehle vitt ayog ne rajyon ke vittiya adhikaar badhaane kaa safar shuru kar diya tha, modi ne yojana ayog ko khatm karte hue ise manzil tak pahunchaa diya
 a new blueprint of federalism is emerging in India with the first full budget of the Modi government, in which the power-rich center will now be weak, while the states will become a new force in financial matters and the development needs are now not only from Delhi but also Jaipur, Bhopal, Lucknow, Chennai will also be from Bangalore, Kolkata, who have to develop this new financial strength and capabilities to handle independence
 jetali kaa bhaashan sunne ke baad bhi aap in baton se hai anjaan?yojana ayog ko khatm karte hue narendra modi vikendrikrut aarthik niti niyojan kaa nayaa khaakaa bhale hi spasht na kar paae hon lekin unhone aarthik sansadhano ke bantwaare main centre ke dabadabe ko jarur khatm kar diya
 The fourteenth Finance Commission has done the remaining work
 bajet se pehle isaki jo report sarkaar ne sweekaar kii he vah centre va rajyon ke vittiya rishton kaa nakshaa badalane ja rahi he

 ravivaar ko The name of the book - Bhaag Milkha Bhaaglekha - Milkha Singh's Writings - Sonia Samwalkaprakash - Prabhat Prakashan Price - Rs 125 (paperback) Both 'bhaag Milkha Bhaag' and 'milkha Singh' do not need introduction

 So the process of turning the pages of the book started and in the first lines that i saw, it was written - If you want to destroy the celebrity, then there is gul-e-gulzar in Dana Khak
 yah kitaab kii shuruyaat main bhoomika se bhi pehle ankit kii gai panktiyaan hai

 milkha singh ne kitaab ke 20wein adhyay 'upsanhaar' main likhaa he, 'main na to koi lekhak hum or na hi rachayita balki ek jununee khilaadi hum, jisane is kitaab main apana dil kholkar rakh diya he
 'believe me if you read the book, you also feel the same
 asal main yah kitaab milkha singh ke ehsaas, unke vichaar or unke yah vichaar kaise bane isi kii baangi he

 kitaab padhane ke kram main kabhi yah nahin lagata ki aap kisi mahaan hasti kii aatmakatha pard rahe hai
 Turning the pages is like Milkha Singh sitting in front and telling you the result of life in pure desi style
 apane dil kaa haal saamne rakh rahe hai
 What's new in the book is the basis of the film 'bhaag Milkha Bhaag' and the autobiography 'bhaag Milkha Bhaag', but the style and design are different
 masalan kitaab main aisi kai baaten yaa kahaniyaan hai jo film main nahin dikhaai gai hai or kitaab padhakar yah jaankaree milti he ki film main aise kai tathy the jo asal main sirf manoranjan ke put ke taur par istemaal kiye gaye the

 Dil Ki Baat Milkha Singh has divided his life into 20 chapters
 inamen kai adhyay aise hai, jisamen unhone vaaki dil kholkar rakh diya he
